netty-javadoc in fedora-34

This page displays detail informations of the netty-javadoc package. You might want go back to the main page of netty-javadoc.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2021-01-26 Fedora Release Engineering - 4.1.51-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_34_Mass_Rebuild
2020-09-07 Mat Booth - 4.1.51-1 - Update to latest upstream version - Native bits were not used by anything, so package is now noarch
2020-07-28 Fedora Release Engineering - 4.1.13-19 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_33_Mass_Rebuild
2020-07-24 Mat Booth - 4.1.13-18 - Don't ship the bundled all-in-one jar - Fix java 11 build
2020-07-11 Jiri Vanek - 4.1.13-17 - Rebuilt for JDK-11, see https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Changes/Java11
2020-06-30 Jeff Johnston - 4.1.13-16 - add BR for Java 1.8.0 and set macro which can later be set to Java 11
2020-03-27 Mat Booth - 4.1.13-15 - Disable JIT'd builds on arm 32 temporarily due to segfault in JDK, see bug 1818078
2020-01-29 Fedora Release Engineering - 4.1.13-14 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2019-11-21 Fabio Valentini - 4.1.13-13 - Remove unnecessary dependency on parent POM.
2019-07-25 Fedora Release Engineering - 4.1.13-12 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_31_Mass_Rebuild
